	<utterance id="1670">
		How to Survive Heart Attack when alone !!! Let's say it's 6.15 p m and you're going home ( alone of course ) , after an unusually hard day on the job . You're really tired , upset and frustrated . Suddenly you start experiencing severe pain in your chest that starts to adiate out into your arm and up into your jaw . You are only about five miles from the hospital nearest your home . Unfortunately you don't know if you'll be able to make it that far . You have been trained in CPR , but the guy that taught the course did not tell you how to perform it on yourself . HOW TO SURVIVE A HEART ATTACK WHEN ALONE Since many people are alone when they suffer a heart attack , without help , the person whose heart is beating improperly and who begins to feel faint , has only about 10 seconds left before losing consciousness . However , these victims can help themselves by coughing repeatedly and very vigorously . A deep breath should be taken before each cough , and the cough must be deep and prolonged , as when producing sputum from deep inside the chest . A breath and a cough must be repeated about every two seconds without let-up until help arrives , or until the heart is felt to be beating normally again . Deep breaths get oxygen into the lungs and coughing movements squeeze the heart and keep the blood circulating . The squeezing pressure on the heart also helps it regain normal rhythm . In this way , heart attack victims can get to a hospital . Tell as many other people as possible about this . It could save their lives !! A cardiologist says If everyone who gets this info shares it with 10 people , you can bet that we'll save at least one life .

	<utterance id="2504">
		Note to the readers : If anyone is not fond of long posts kindly refrain from reading it .. :) Exact date ta mone nei . 2010 er November er kotha . Raat around 11:30 hobe , ami Jadavpur train station theke neme pray 15 min opekha kore ekta Rickshaw ke besi taka diye hire kore barir dike jachi . Ami firchilam Dumdum theke , amar ex girlfriend er bari okhane . Tar bari thekei firchilam , deri kore beriechilam tai metro na peye train e firte holo . Sei samayta chilo khub jotil , onek chap bolte ja bojhai tai nite hochilo . Job er bivinno jhamela to chiloi tar sathe chilo arekti boro chap . Tar sathe relationship ta thikthak cholchilo nah coz tar life er past complications amader relationship e eshe porechilo . Sedin o jhogra hoyechilo , tai ami iche kore late kore berai so dat she mite feel my support and love for her and our relationship comes back to normal . Sedin amar bag e ekta rum er neep chilo , TRain e ashte ashte seta kheye ni n eet . :P Nyways , amar bari jadavpur theke khub ekta beshi durotte nah , station theke rickshaw niye jete borojor half n hour lage . So rickshaw te uthe ekta cigarette dhorie besh sukhtan marte marte jachi ami barir dike . Rickshaw takhan JU'r first gate er samne , hothat ekti meye khub tarahuro kore amar rickshaw ti ke haath dekhai . Ami chalok ke boli rickshaw thamate . Meyeti hapate hapate eshe bole " Can u give me a lift . If not the whole way atleast 8b porjonto coz m pretty late and barir loke chinta korche . " Ami take uthe ashte boli . Meyetir sathe ekta boro plastic vorti prochur papers and khata ache notice korlam . Meyeti khub dekhte misti and simple . Kothabarta khub vodro nomro . tini porone chilen ekti blue tanktop , a blue maidwaist denim , hairs tied up in a ponytail , and on her eyes . Khub forsha rong and jehetu onek hepa soite hoyechilo onake tai she was a bit sweaty , but the mixed aroma of her sweat and her deo was amazing . ( Tar feeling ta ektu pore realize kori :P ) .. Nyways so flash forward to the future , 8b te rickshaw pouchalo and to her amazement sekhane ekta rickshaw to durer kotha ekta auto nei . Meyeti rickshaw te otha porjonto amar sarthe ar kono kotha hoyni , so oi scene dekhe I broke the ice first and asked her je " Apni thaken kothay ? " . Meyeti khub gombhir vabe bollo je se thake Bansdroni . Ami take boli je ami bansdronir kichu agei thaki so jehetu eki route tai ami bari porjonto chole giye onake rickshaw ti diye debo and uni bari porjonto pouche jaben . Rickshaw chalok o beshi takar lov e raji hoye gelo , and she also agreed on my proposition . Jete jete we started talkin to each other . Ami arekta cigarette dhorie kotha bolchilam tar sathe . Cigarette er smoke and the stale smell of alcohol ta tar nake lagay tini nakh kuchkalen ami seta notice kore cigarette ta feledilam , Pocket e luckily ekta happydent chilo , seta mukhe pure chibate laglam . seta dekhe ekta halka smile dilo meyeta . vebechilo je ami notice korbona but ami notice korechi dekhe halka blush kore mukhti onno dike sorye nilo . kotha bole janlam je meyeti JU te Economics hons . niye porche . ( Takhan tini 2nd yr e ) , xam er age project miliye aro notes photocopy korte korte tar eto late hoye geche . Meyeti G.D. Birla theke higher secondary passout kore ju te economics niye porche , tar baba SBI er ekti branch e kaj koren . Amake jiggesh kore ami kotha theke ashchilam ami keno janina sotti kothata na bole bole feli je ekta ofc er colleague er barite party chilo , Okhan theke firchilam . Amar kajer bepare jiggesh kore ami boli ami kothay job kori , and then aro discussions hote hote amra egiye chollam . Rastar dhare kichu moddop jubok maramari korche dekhe meyeti chup kore gutishuti hoye boshe roilo mukh nichu kore . Amio silently tar pashe boshe chilam ar majhe majhe ar chokhe dekhcilam take . Se ta bujhte pere meyeti jakhan i takachilo ami mukh firiye nichilam . bujhte parchilam meyeti chupti kore hashche . Kothay ache nah je valo muhurto gulo chokher poloke chole jai , realise korlam tai hote choleche . Rickshaw amar barir khub kacha kachi . Ami kichu na vebe hothat take bole feli je " You know what I cannot let you go alone in this hr of night . " Meyeti hotovombo hoye chokh gol gol kore bole " Mane ? " Ami khub santo hoye or chokhe dike takye boli je " dekhun eto raat e apnar eka ei rasta diye jaoa uchit na . So what i am proposing is je apni amar sathe amar barir samne neme porun and ami rickshaw ke taka diye tata kore di , and then ami apnake bike e kore chere diye ashbo . Amar bepare kono sondeho rakhben na mone , I promise you i will drop u home safely widout a single scratch on u . " Meyeti koyekmuhurto amar chokher dike takiye raji hoye jai . Ekta halka dai , You know oi " I trust you " kinda smile . Rickshaw ke amar barir kichu age chere diye ami take ekti jaigai bosiye rekhe boli 2 min opekha korun ami bike niye ashchi . Ami pagoler moto dourre barir theke biker chabi niye bike ber kore tar kache chole ashi hapate hapate . Amake sei obosthay meyeti dekhe jei vabe takalo oi muhurto ta was wow , As if it was out of this world . Bike e othar samay amake jiggesh kore je kivabe bosbo , ami boli jetate apni comfortable feel koren , seta sune meyeti ekside hoye boshlo . Tar hath ti tini prothome amar kadhe rakhen . Bike cholte shuru kore , ami oti aste aste bike chaliye take tar barir uddeshe niye jete thaki . rastay majhe phone ashe tar . Meyetir baba phone kore jante chai kothay ache and joldi ashte , Meyeti bole 10 min pouche jabe . Ami speed ta ektu high kori bike er and meyeti tar kadh amar kadh theke soriye rakhe amar komor e Amar kadhe halka kore tar mathata rekhe dei . 10 min er agei ami take tar barir samne pouche di , Dekhi tar baba darye achen flat er baire . Amake dekhe uni ektu rege jaan but meyeti sob bujhye bolate he thanked me and tar no neoar kotha bole . Tini bolen je ekdin tar barite ashte . Edike amar barir theke fone korche ei janar janno je ami eto raat e bari te eshe abar bike niye kothay berolam , Tai ami onar no ta jus sune nilam , cell e save korar kothata matha te asheni ar . Amar chokh takhan meyetir dike , Meyeti tar babar pechone darye amake dekhe jache , Babar sathe jaoar age meyeti amar hatha dhore shake hand kore Hashi mukhe thank you bole and chole jai . ami darye darye tar jaoa dekhi bisonno chitte . flat er gate er dhokar age meyeti fire amar dike takay and ek mukh hashi diye nije arale chole jai . Dekha hoa and chere deoar muhurto porjonto bolte gele amar gf er kotha amar mathatei asheni . Nyways tarpor ami bari chole ashi . Eshe bujhte pari ki blunder tai na korechi . Meyetir babar no ta matha thekei berye geche . Meyetir babao amar no niyechilen , I hoped je hoyto meyetir baba othoba meyeti nije amake ekbarer janno holeo call korbe , but etodine ami tar ekta call o paini . P.S. : Admin and baki pathok pathikara hoyto vabchen je keno eto boro ekta post likhte gelam ami . Actually ei ghotonar 3 bochor poreo aguntik muhurter moton ajkeo hothat sei meyetir kotha mone pore gelo . Take ami ar konodin dekhini . 2011 r february te amar breakup hoy . Tar por ami onekbar somaye oshomaye tar flat er baire diye gechi take ekbar dekhar janno tar sathe kichu muhurto kotha bolar janno but sei souvaggo ar hoyni . J akhani eka thaki ba ektu mushre pori tar mukhti mone pore jai and I feel alive again . che kore ontoto ekbar janar janno je se valo ache kina , se sukhe ache kina . Majhe majhe mone hoi kothao na kothao amar ar sei meyetir story osompurno theke jai . Rum er emon i mohan kripa je Meyetir naam o mone nei , je take fb te ontoto khuje ber korbo . Ei post ta korchi ekta chotto hope niye je hoyto se konodin konovabe ei post ti porben and ekti reply onoto deben .. Pathok pathika der uddeshe ekta chotto request je jodi konodin apnar bandhobir kach theke ei same story sune thaken and jodi tar details ei post er songe mele kindly take ektibar post ti porar kotha bolben . Apatoto ami chakri chere JU'r student . Master korchi JU theke . Majhe majhe free hole economics dept er samne diye pass kori in case jodi take dekhte pai . Nyways ar bore korbona apnader . Have a grt time everybody . Take care and godbless u all . ItsybitsySpider ....

Although I arrived very late in your life when you had many responsibilities in your head but they never hampered you in loving me . You showered me with whatever you had and still showering your love upon me like rain . You had put a lot of effort in upbringing me . You always fulfilled my every small demand without questioning . Once I heard you were saying to mom , \ " If sometimes meal falls short , even then give full plate to babu , You and I can manage but he should not feel crisis . \ " It touched me dad . You purchased me a laptop even when you were having monetary issues , a Galaxy S Advance , clothes for every occasion and hefty schools fees . I know dad , you were never so rich , but still never denied and managed every minute demand of mine . You always provided me with enough pocket money to sustain for month . I know you have a blind faith on me that's why you never influenced me in taking my decisions about my studies , streams , subjects etc . But dad , I still didn't proved it to you . Dad just bless me for not breaking your faith . And I'll prove it to you one fine day that all your hard work , sheer dedication , perseverance didn't went futile .
